## Frontend changes

Add the fetch interceptor script to all protected admin pages, or once in the shared admin base template if all those pages extend it, because the protected admin pages are the dashboard, billing, history, settings, tenants, archive, and backups pages. The interceptor must watch for `401` or `403` plus the `X-Session-Expired: 1` header, then redirect to `X-Redirect-Url`, because the current app otherwise leaves the stale page open and only fails when the next secured fetch occurs. ## Routes affected

Admin PDF routes use `get_current_admin_api()`, so they are part of the bug and will start redirecting correctly after the middleware change instead of showing raw unauthorized output. Tenant KYC upload, tenant KYC inactive/delete, and tenant public KYC file view all use `get_current_tenant()`, so they are also covered by the tenant middleware patch. Protected admin routers are mounted under `/admin` with page protection and API protection separated, which is why visible pages can remain open while later API actions fail independently. Tenant auth cookies also use a separate access-cookie path under `/t`, which is why tenant public pages need their own redirect handling rather than reusing the admin flow. ## Validation steps

After applying the patch, test admin like this:
1. Log in to admin.
2. Open dashboard or billing.
3. Wait until access token expiry, or manually invalidate the session row.
4. Click a PDF view/download or any API-backed action.
5. Confirm the app redirects through admin logout/login instead of showing `"Unauthorized"`. Test tenant like this:
1. Open a tenant public profile link and authenticate.
2. Wait until expiry, or revoke the tenant session.
3. Try KYC upload/delete or open a tenant KYC file.
4. Confirm the page redirects back to the tenant public profile re-auth flow instead of showing `"Access token expired. Requires refresh."` or `"Unauthorized"`. ## Optional cleanup

Your admin and tenant cookie helpers already provide cookie clearing functions, and the tenant auth router includes logout endpoints, so no extra cookie-layer redesign is required for this fix. ## Target architecture

Use a React app for the admin panel and tenant portal, while FastAPI continues to own business logic, auth cookies, files, PDF generation, imports/exports, backups, and database access. The current backend already exposes strong API coverage for tenants, billing, settings, backups, sync/import-export, WhatsApp, PDFs, health checks, and tenant KYC flows, so the backend mostly needs contract cleanup rather than a redesign. Recommended structure:
- `frontend/admin-app`: React admin SPA.
- `frontend/tenant-app`: React tenant portal SPA, or a single SPA with route groups.
- FastAPI serves APIs under `/api`, tenant auth under `/api/auth`, and can serve built frontend assets after migration.
- Keep cookie auth, because the app already uses HttpOnly admin and tenant access/refresh cookies with refresh rotation and session tables. ## Backend changes

Add JSON endpoints for session bootstrap, because admin login currently uses an HTML login page at `/login` plus form POST `/api/login`, and the tenant public page currently depends on HTML page rendering at `/t/{view_token}` with PIN-based unlock flow. Suggested new endpoints:
- `GET /api/admin/me` → current admin session info.
- `POST /api/admin/login` → JSON login alternative to the current form flow.
- `POST /api/admin/logout` → JSON logout alternative to the current redirect logout.
- `POST /api/admin/refresh` or reuse `/api/refresh` carefully for admin only.
- `GET /api/dashboard` → dashboard stats JSON.
- `GET /api/tenant/me` → current tenant session info after PIN login.
- `GET /api/public/tenant/{view_token}` → public tenant bootstrap payload for the portal page. ## React routes

The current page system maps cleanly into React routes because your app already has distinct pages for dashboard, billing, history, tenants, settings, archive, backups, tenant profile, and tenant public profile. ## Frontend structure

Use React Router, TanStack Query, and a small API client with `credentials: "include"` on every request, because your authentication model depends on cookies scoped to `/admin`, `/t`, and `/api/auth`. [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/83904925/d31a7d6a-ed8c-4dfb-9bae-a1aa794ba0bb/rent.md?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYE3DO76TYA&Signature=yw7Z6oq85VUUJ%2F8WRz%2BJL%2FWmGtA%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEJz%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJHMEUCIFOrrbHpJdhFwuitoxhU4EaltqJ72%2BHpJT0tfDKag%2BPOAiEA8InaX%2FXKae8QW%2BG81WdhqHC4qEOGKuWCth%2FWDROWkZEq8wQIZRABGgw2OTk3NTMzMDk3MDUiDOsYjeu8sNr4wVe3byrQBJfkpAQp%2FBKBSm%2BwIt2eUq10YYOmt62dkCnPjp8MdXiJI2QneAgD8NkS%2BbjQQsfNRqEcmMHhh7nE89Vdf%2FFv0N%2Ff7cqiNCo6M9R4W3i1iu8h3umQJMkwUtQOrejW%2FnIFvPMl92L%2FghfOxk3gPVhLVxrLH2YwCTw0qQUmJK9j4AMUqL5HIDvC2R5RmAJ8%2BVC68n3b38Xn2qSGUSs02G%2FBuLcTE3zmaByogC8GO%2BdtOjAvlx9AOrhkIKPTIxhQWRG59vff3S7%2Fy%2BwlNjTySZRIO%2BEvzDa3mlJ8zaFFJaQ7IHR99pJ6r0cD5mKJU7Krvug5zJz35zYuf6f08W1F2EMPlXBlkQDDgh9UFdmVjkRZh9ShBp6FYaIjw3b2t1nS%2Bl3Ssm6NA32zPeQpSl9we3FaxJKGabS6CWqazFi%2B1Sl%2F%2ByM4hD%2Fqg8UcUoQ%2BpLFbFoX16%2BdDIkp95bCW4yrj%2F8ymX4jUBNhZl1tbElIvc6tgBPG7YTR4UIDZWtc7Tirm1TfgSfe%2BkRBzBQ1lxGC0szdUxCJriZrWUrDk4DZMHqpwDCRtRSwr%2F7uqpdO%2Bm8ZzQdmV9gIGkkuUI4erIp43a3pP3Kn9LGKN8XhxXuKe3vTKghKlgh5heFls4xXmHLOTGEkxN4n1dGMcHyedt8V37LahPE0xrXR3XR8Dtcs45BUgLVZ2QdVmjbKhtZVNZSFzpP6qtXCD%2FgZGHKeRzGZJs5UluAWV2a5v01HeC4I0P%2B2q2G5J0lbInAeikTyHjNip%2FsuEt335qNi4JC%2BfLHK7QoIUWegwxfCx0gY6mAFww10%2F6iqPvj93lJ5Tbkv%2FMJ15hkhTgkhrx6wQTFWjgaWh%2FtcBMEvvj8OV8hfK%2BYDskIEiQpwSLg%2FEvavXxnT97PVhFLTQqM3Lj6jL%2F7%2BV66YuhvzFjqDQIHHuGR0fK%2Bcc31a%2BbC0MFrzBZE6y1c%2BRYbncFBBzNNos71Aoj76AXY7wQxE38h%2FD3p8kti7yaziqo9vLrlmqOA%3D%3D&Expires=1783399960)
Build around layouts and feature modules instead of page-specific script blobs, since the current UI logic is spread across individual HTML templates and that is the main maintainability problem you are trying to remove. ## UX improvements

A React migration is the right time to improve flows that are clunky in server-rendered pages: billing preview can become real-time, tenant and receipt tables can get client-side filters with server refresh, KYC uploads can show progress and previews, and backup/import actions can use modal confirmations with clearer result states. The current backend already supports these operations individually, but the HTML architecture limits responsiveness and state handling. [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/83904925/d31a7d6a-ed8c-4dfb-9bae-a1aa794ba0bb/rent.md?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYE3DO76TYA&Signature=yw7Z6oq85VUUJ%2F8WRz%2BJL%2FWmGtA%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEJz%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJHMEUCIFOrrbHpJdhFwuitoxhU4EaltqJ72%2BHpJT0tfDKag%2BPOAiEA8InaX%2FXKae8QW%2BG81WdhqHC4qEOGKuWCth%2FWDROWkZEq8wQIZRABGgw2OTk3NTMzMDk3MDUiDOsYjeu8sNr4wVe3byrQBJfkpAQp%2FBKBSm%2BwIt2eUq10YYOmt62dkCnPjp8MdXiJI2QneAgD8NkS%2BbjQQsfNRqEcmMHhh7nE89Vdf%2FFv0N%2Ff7cqiNCo6M9R4W3i1iu8h3umQJMkwUtQOrejW%2FnIFvPMl92L%2FghfOxk3gPVhLVxrLH2YwCTw0qQUmJK9j4AMUqL5HIDvC2R5RmAJ8%2BVC68n3b38Xn2qSGUSs02G%2FBuLcTE3zmaByogC8GO%2BdtOjAvlx9AOrhkIKPTIxhQWRG59vff3S7%2Fy%2BwlNjTySZRIO%2BEvzDa3mlJ8zaFFJaQ7IHR99pJ6r0cD5mKJU7Krvug5zJz35zYuf6f08W1F2EMPlXBlkQDDgh9UFdmVjkRZh9ShBp6FYaIjw3b2t1nS%2Bl3Ssm6NA32zPeQpSl9we3FaxJKGabS6CWqazFi%2B1Sl%2F%2ByM4hD%2Fqg8UcUoQ%2BpLFbFoX16%2BdDIkp95bCW4yrj%2F8ymX4jUBNhZl1tbElIvc6tgBPG7YTR4UIDZWtc7Tirm1TfgSfe%2BkRBzBQ1lxGC0szdUxCJriZrWUrDk4DZMHqpwDCRtRSwr%2F7uqpdO%2Bm8ZzQdmV9gIGkkuUI4erIp43a3pP3Kn9LGKN8XhxXuKe3vTKghKlgh5heFls4xXmHLOTGEkxN4n1dGMcHyedt8V37LahPE0xrXR3XR8Dtcs45BUgLVZ2QdVmjbKhtZVNZSFzpP6qtXCD%2FgZGHKeRzGZJs5UluAWV2a5v01HeC4I0P%2B2q2G5J0lbInAeikTyHjNip%2FsuEt335qNi4JC%2BfLHK7QoIUWegwxfCx0gY6mAFww10%2F6iqPvj93lJ5Tbkv%2FMJ15hkhTgkhrx6wQTFWjgaWh%2FtcBMEvvj8OV8hfK%2BYDskIEiQpwSLg%2FEvavXxnT97PVhFLTQqM3Lj6jL%2F7%2BV66YuhvzFjqDQIHHuGR0fK%2Bcc31a%2BbC0MFrzBZE6y1c%2BRYbncFBBzNNos71Aoj76AXY7wQxE38h%2FD3p8kti7yaziqo9vLrlmqOA%3D%3D&Expires=1783399960)

High-impact UX upgrades:
- Global session-expiry interceptor using the existing `X-Session-Expired` and `X-Redirect-Url` headers. - Lazy-loaded admin sections.
- Reusable tables with sorting, filtering, row actions.
- Draft-preserving forms for billing/settings.
- Upload progress for signature and KYC files.
- Skeleton loaders instead of full-page refreshes.
- Better mobile navigation than the current template-per-page approach. ## Migration phases

Do this in phases, not as a big-bang rewrite, because the backend already mixes page routes and API routes and you can keep the business logic stable while swapping the UI layer. The current page routes are `/`, `/billing`, `/history`, `/tenants`, `/settings`, `/archive`, `/backups`, and `/t/{view_token}`, so those can be replaced gradually by React entry points while existing APIs remain live. [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/83904925/d31a7d6a-ed8c-4dfb-9bae-a1aa794ba0bb/rent.md?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYE3DO76TYA&Signature=yw7Z6oq85VUUJ%2F8WRz%2BJL%2FWmGtA%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEJz%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJHMEUCIFOrrbHpJdhFwuitoxhU4EaltqJ72%2BHpJT0tfDKag%2BPOAiEA8InaX%2FXKae8QW%2BG81WdhqHC4qEOGKuWCth%2FWDROWkZEq8wQIZRABGgw2OTk3NTMzMDk3MDUiDOsYjeu8sNr4wVe3byrQBJfkpAQp%2FBKBSm%2BwIt2eUq10YYOmt62dkCnPjp8MdXiJI2QneAgD8NkS%2BbjQQsfNRqEcmMHhh7nE89Vdf%2FFv0N%2Ff7cqiNCo6M9R4W3i1iu8h3umQJMkwUtQOrejW%2FnIFvPMl92L%2FghfOxk3gPVhLVxrLH2YwCTw0qQUmJK9j4AMUqL5HIDvC2R5RmAJ8%2BVC68n3b38Xn2qSGUSs02G%2FBuLcTE3zmaByogC8GO%2BdtOjAvlx9AOrhkIKPTIxhQWRG59vff3S7%2Fy%2BwlNjTySZRIO%2BEvzDa3mlJ8zaFFJaQ7IHR99pJ6r0cD5mKJU7Krvug5zJz35zYuf6f08W1F2EMPlXBlkQDDgh9UFdmVjkRZh9ShBp6FYaIjw3b2t1nS%2Bl3Ssm6NA32zPeQpSl9we3FaxJKGabS6CWqazFi%2B1Sl%2F%2ByM4hD%2Fqg8UcUoQ%2BpLFbFoX16%2BdDIkp95bCW4yrj%2F8ymX4jUBNhZl1tbElIvc6tgBPG7YTR4UIDZWtc7Tirm1TfgSfe%2BkRBzBQ1lxGC0szdUxCJriZrWUrDk4DZMHqpwDCRtRSwr%2F7uqpdO%2Bm8ZzQdmV9gIGkkuUI4erIp43a3pP3Kn9LGKN8XhxXuKe3vTKghKlgh5heFls4xXmHLOTGEkxN4n1dGMcHyedt8V37LahPE0xrXR3XR8Dtcs45BUgLVZ2QdVmjbKhtZVNZSFzpP6qtXCD%2FgZGHKeRzGZJs5UluAWV2a5v01HeC4I0P%2B2q2G5J0lbInAeikTyHjNip%2FsuEt335qNi4JC%2BfLHK7QoIUWegwxfCx0gY6mAFww10%2F6iqPvj93lJ5Tbkv%2FMJ15hkhTgkhrx6wQTFWjgaWh%2FtcBMEvvj8OV8hfK%2BYDskIEiQpwSLg%2FEvavXxnT97PVhFLTQqM3Lj6jL%2F7%2BV66YuhvzFjqDQIHHuGR0fK%2Bcc31a%2BbC0MFrzBZE6y1c%2BRYbncFBBzNNos71Aoj76AXY7wQxE38h%2FD3p8kti7yaziqo9vLrlmqOA%3D%3D&Expires=1783399960)

Recommended rollout:
1. Add new JSON auth/bootstrap endpoints.
2. Build shared React API layer with cookie/session handling.
3. Migrate admin login and dashboard first.
4. Migrate billing and history next, since they already rely heavily on APIs. 5. Migrate tenants, settings, archive, backups.

7. Remove Jinja page templates after parity is verified. My recommendation is:
- React + TypeScript
- Vite
- TanStack Query
- React Router
- Zod + React Hook Form
- a component system such as shadcn/ui or MUI
- keep FastAPI cookies exactly as the auth boundary. Yes — below is a concrete implementation pack for replacing the current template-based frontend with React while preserving the existing FastAPI business logic, auth, files, PDFs, backups, and tenant flows. The present system already has page templates such as `dashboard.html`, `billing.html`, `history.html`, `tenants.html`, `settings.html`, `archive.html`, `backups.html`, `tenant_public_profile.html`, and `admin_login.html`, plus strong API coverage under `/api` and `/api/auth`, so this is a frontend-first migration rather than a backend rewrite. ## Architecture

The clean target is a React admin SPA mounted under `/admin` and a React tenant portal under `/t/:viewToken`, while FastAPI continues to handle auth cookies, billing logic, tenants, KYC, backups, sync/import-export, WhatsApp link generation, and PDF/file responses. [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/83904925/d31a7d6a-ed8c-4dfb-9bae-a1aa794ba0bb/rent.md?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYE6EEBDYTD&Signature=dMyaK2Evx4xsqVM9ImJOzxyQZac%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEJz%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJIMEYCIQCU2vkqSw6MKoUWTLw9KZxU5TsiLCYVO0RoKaFt2qlimQIhAN2lpC086AX9K2T7yhFABr3fm1v1yFRelEHbOF7ycW%2FAKvMECGUQARoMNjk5NzUzMzA5NzA1IgxLtWcCcx36pMYdFMIq0ATvS4cSypQAI5fSu8%2F9PQk1NCAXIEk5VT%2BvkojqLkqc%2BHkMeOrYDAM0JpBHBTGuWFGSM87pNoAGkP9xMXMzMIS5MF2YlATD4eLqK9LuxZ9RM%2BWaTtKLhY1fY4bzi%2FQzejgRdTzu9mIeHXKc38UcEUD3c%2BqLYQGRYoGIJXKR%2B0E2WC5cp2L9cD3E711sZsArxi2Igwmy3uXVusqnNq6mjb0yY8XiVOLj4wLH%2B4CniouPYw9nQcjwAPMbgjhQfefW66K55yep2Q0eCUu5MeDqaMsc9D22TiJGLMGMSZ3u6efrM3tTVbgc%2Bi5CbppSlCMKD8dSDxRddOK9A3uQgcXJt%2Bnrw88Ic5bwiE6EdV%2BZBf7KNJfBLaEAOJc8Bz274aVTp06oDxbmieF1daQU%2B5HojcbrAQenDyBiP58I2a%2FhOTwldOmsB7i6SxIPOVvUjCdvtSfw9kiLlVVEqtZoWK%2Bh%2BOOypDAJ3wqjgBit6F1EVxraQD6u%2B9CwmTxMAitHFl93IiK0dNtP2VLXuIbTDOupeC9vAH0dlnWG0C%2FKCp9sTBczWSPJGf1JiUdIObOmwtedVFCvkH4KWKWmR%2FwHd1SGlM7xlyoshfY8GY7%2FyGsAeFcN45PGuFnh0OknkRbHrn%2Fmz1ACkJabMJ%2BIji4Tk%2BMx%2FNob2UGwDA%2BUviyGoluPX78TUApA7UZTSuxVMPj4gDnHHQUtgS8%2F1zvBzARnEYIdCxXDp0%2F5n60t%2BqjKDzeugpv8FF3GIIoO4Dlj50oZjrTIs1bYJVF57RJ%2FwFO9meBHLAQsMMDysdIGOpcBL6bGjoMvw1iY%2BPtPeXi%2F1VsNwDN5U9eRQUCKZ%2FP7q%2BX%2BwzlVJofwhIq8deEeFCxlABH53lHQnjXU%2FXKYtr4oVqNn9jWr6lslDHXog7P2t8APPyPrpZfhYYTXGjC9pF8r6tMVi42ufa6esJ%2FdqiFu6PmNytv1aX5pybQAaXx0xd%2B10gzlEkWVhUw7105lv5oiZJnL2obbQw%3D%3D&Expires=1783400211)

Recommended app split:
```text
frontend/
  admin-app/
    src/
      app/
      features/
      components/
      layouts/
      pages/
      lib/
  tenant-app/
    src/
      app/
      features/
      components/
      layouts/
      pages/
      lib/

backend/
  app/
    api/
    authentication/
    pages/
    routers/
    services/
    core/
```

## Folder tree

Your current backend separates API routers like `api/billing.py`, `api/tenants.py`, `api/settings.py`, `api/backup.py`, `api/pdf.py`, `api/public.py`, and `routers/auth.py`, so the React apps should mirror those domains as frontend feature modules rather than page-specific scripts. ## Route map

The current page routes are legacy-admin oriented, with redirects from `/dashboard`, `/billing`, `/history`, `/tenants`, `/settings`, `/archive`, `/backups`, and `/login` into `/admin/...`, while tenant public access is built around `/t/{view_token}`. ## API contracts

Most admin data APIs are already React-ready because they return JSON or file streams, including billing, tenants, settings, backups, sync, WhatsApp, PDF, and tenant KYC endpoints. [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/83904925/d31a7d6a-ed8c-4dfb-9bae-a1aa794ba0bb/rent.md?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYE6EEBDYTD&Signature=dMyaK2Evx4xsqVM9ImJOzxyQZac%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEJz%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJIMEYCIQCU2vkqSw6MKoUWTLw9KZxU5TsiLCYVO0RoKaFt2qlimQIhAN2lpC086AX9K2T7yhFABr3fm1v1yFRelEHbOF7ycW%2FAKvMECGUQARoMNjk5NzUzMzA5NzA1IgxLtWcCcx36pMYdFMIq0ATvS4cSypQAI5fSu8%2F9PQk1NCAXIEk5VT%2BvkojqLkqc%2BHkMeOrYDAM0JpBHBTGuWFGSM87pNoAGkP9xMXMzMIS5MF2YlATD4eLqK9LuxZ9RM%2BWaTtKLhY1fY4bzi%2FQzejgRdTzu9mIeHXKc38UcEUD3c%2BqLYQGRYoGIJXKR%2B0E2WC5cp2L9cD3E711sZsArxi2Igwmy3uXVusqnNq6mjb0yY8XiVOLj4wLH%2B4CniouPYw9nQcjwAPMbgjhQfefW66K55yep2Q0eCUu5MeDqaMsc9D22TiJGLMGMSZ3u6efrM3tTVbgc%2Bi5CbppSlCMKD8dSDxRddOK9A3uQgcXJt%2Bnrw88Ic5bwiE6EdV%2BZBf7KNJfBLaEAOJc8Bz274aVTp06oDxbmieF1daQU%2B5HojcbrAQenDyBiP58I2a%2FhOTwldOmsB7i6SxIPOVvUjCdvtSfw9kiLlVVEqtZoWK%2Bh%2BOOypDAJ3wqjgBit6F1EVxraQD6u%2B9CwmTxMAitHFl93IiK0dNtP2VLXuIbTDOupeC9vAH0dlnWG0C%2FKCp9sTBczWSPJGf1JiUdIObOmwtedVFCvkH4KWKWmR%2FwHd1SGlM7xlyoshfY8GY7%2FyGsAeFcN45PGuFnh0OknkRbHrn%2Fmz1ACkJabMJ%2BIji4Tk%2BMx%2FNob2UGwDA%2BUviyGoluPX78TUApA7UZTSuxVMPj4gDnHHQUtgS8%2F1zvBzARnEYIdCxXDp0%2F5n60t%2BqjKDzeugpv8FF3GIIoO4Dlj50oZjrTIs1bYJVF57RJ%2FwFO9meBHLAQsMMDysdIGOpcBL6bGjoMvw1iY%2BPtPeXi%2F1VsNwDN5U9eRQUCKZ%2FP7q%2BX%2BwzlVJofwhIq8deEeFCxlABH53lHQnjXU%2FXKYtr4oVqNn9jWr6lslDHXog7P2t8APPyPrpZfhYYTXGjC9pF8r6tMVi42ufa6esJ%2FdqiFu6PmNytv1aX5pybQAaXx0xd%2B10gzlEkWVhUw7105lv5oiZJnL2obbQw%3D%3D&Expires=1783400211)
The main gaps are session-bootstrap and page-bootstrap endpoints, because admin login is still tied to page redirects and tenant public entry still depends on server-rendered HTML plus PIN unlock. Add these first JSON contracts:

| Endpoint | Purpose | Why needed |
|---|---|---|
| `GET /api/admin/me` | Return current admin identity and session summary. | Admin auth currently uses cookies plus middleware, but React needs a bootstrap endpoint for route guards and refresh recovery. ## First endpoints

The first backend pass should add only the missing JSON bootstrap layer and leave the rest of the Python code untouched, because most operational APIs already exist and work. Start with admin session endpoints, tenant bootstrap endpoints, and dashboard JSON, then build the React API client around `credentials: "include"` so it works with the existing cookie paths for admin under `/admin` and tenant refresh under `/api/auth`. Suggested first FastAPI additions:
```python
# routers/admin_auth_api.py
from fastapi import APIRouter, Request, Response, HTTPException, Depends
from pydantic import BaseModel
from app.authentication.admin.cookies import set_admin_auth_cookies, clear_admin_auth_cookies
from app.authentication.admin.jwt import create_admin_access_token, decode_admin_access_token
from app.authentication.admin.sessions import (
    create_admin_session, get_admin_session_db, revoke_admin_session_db
)
from app.authentication.admin.middleware import get_current_admin_api

router = APIRouter(prefix="/api/admin", tags=["Admin Auth"])

class AdminLoginRequest(BaseModel):
    username: str
    password: str
    remember_me: bool = False

@router.get("/me")
async def admin_me(principal = Depends(get_current_admin_api)):
    return {
        "status": "success",
        "user": {
            "id": principal.id,
            "role": principal.role,
            "session_id": principal.session_id,
        }
    }

@router.post("/login")
async def admin_login(payload: AdminLoginRequest, request: Request, response: Response):
    # reuse your existing admin credential validation logic here
    admin_id = 1
    session_id, refresh_token = create_admin_session(admin_id, request, payload.remember_me)
    access_token = create_admin_access_token(admin_id, session_id)
    cookie_val = f"{session_id}:{refresh_token}"
    set_admin_auth_cookies(response, access_token, cookie_val, payload.remember_me, request)
    return {"status": "success"}

@router.post("/logout")
async def admin_logout(request: Request, response: Response):
    token = request.cookies.get("admin_access_token")
    if token:
        try:
            payload = decode_admin_access_token(token)
            revoke_admin_session_db(payload.get("sid"))
        except Exception:
            pass
    clear_admin_auth_cookies(response, request)
    return {"status": "success"}

@router.post("/refresh")
async def admin_refresh(request: Request, response: Response):
    # mirror tenant refresh rotation logic for admin cookies/sessions
    return {"status": "success"}
```

```python
# api/dashboard.py
from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends
from app.authentication.admin.middleware import get_current_admin_api
from app.services.billing_service import get_dashboard_stats

router = APIRouter()

@router.get("/api/dashboard")
async def api_dashboard(principal = Depends(get_current_admin_api)):
    return {
        "status": "success",
        "data": get_dashboard_stats()
    }
```

```python
# api/public_bootstrap.py
from fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException, Depends, Request
from app.authentication.tenant.middleware import get_current_tenant
from app.services.tenant_service import load_tenants, get_occupants
from app.services.billing_service import get_all_receipts

router = APIRouter()

@router.get("/api/public/tenant/{view_token}")
async def public_tenant_bootstrap(view_token: str):
    tenants = load_tenants()
    tenant = next((t for t in tenants if getattr(t, "view_token", "") == view_token), None)
    if not tenant:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Invalid profile link.")
    return {
        "status": "success",
        "tenant": {
            "id": tenant.id,
            "name": tenant.name,
            "view_token": view_token,
            "room_number": getattr(tenant, "room_number", ""),
            "phone": getattr(tenant, "phone", ""),
            "company": getattr(tenant, "company", ""),
            "status": getattr(tenant, "status", ""),
        }
    }

@router.get("/api/auth/me")
async def tenant_me(principal = Depends(get_current_tenant)):
    return {
        "status": "success",
        "user": {
            "id": principal.id,
            "role": principal.role,
            "session_id": principal.session_id,
        }
    }
```

Recommended execution order:
1. Add the 6–7 bootstrap endpoints above.
2. Build `admin-app` with login, auth guard, dashboard, and billing first.
3. Build `tenant-app` with PIN login, receipt list, and KYC upload next.
4. After parity, remove `TemplateResponse` pages one group at a time. ## Admin app starter

Build the admin app first, because most admin features already rely on API endpoints and only the login/dashboard bootstrap still need thin JSON wrappers. The current admin logout flow is a route named `adminlogout` that revokes the admin session and clears cookies before redirecting to the login page, so React should mirror that behavior with a JSON logout endpoint instead of page redirects. [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/83904925/d31a7d6a-ed8c-4dfb-9bae-a1aa794ba0bb/rent.md?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQ2J3LGHX&Signature=ZABz0iM%2FzHysP%2FN4QKfuFzmm%2BT8%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEJz%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJHMEUCIQCmQ9rOzLMXAbpPPJ7AJ5PVf6ecWzFa6KIrLAG5jU6x8gIge1jW9GBfqjLBT0RbT4T47sEn7u%2BXJPU1x6qFMf2cMn0q8wQIZRABGgw2OTk3NTMzMDk3MDUiDDuPDwBdT4vFe7d4iirQBLGFc45QATeCwQMpsDtDb9X2wUfVpHpUno%2B6HM7QMoBV4PXMl5KzbtyjVoRBuhrtduYqMJLedKCWLeretbrsvL9priyr4NxxU6iCGbbDagSySm7TyfMWpPWdQaA9VcGIOhsQbs%2FT%2Fe0tPpFVY7uAZo1zyL0ihnqb5d26YlTBzPQwItwYcLW%2BRRF6C1DaIo6ElESlOy86MHuabKS11cuc83dRsXkXUWQAnDlChosGF9P%2F6adV9ZM%2FMfvAe4YbAuWa0VeYhU9WuyuYepSfBatwCnkvGFWWBaBttO0kCUt%2BPGYnFD7TCgeseMsgTGHBQ8UvBp4o73Uxvc41t%2BcJb8sthKytPTd4mN%2BP%2BEDZlmVteBVffPhu42yPN8s4aw8fspqqS9cSLP9%2Bd5NRnnCRLuLtCtMEBMJnRUZCzuqjb%2FluEkvmTl0xpeaXdRcyLDLZQfQ%2F65PmiwELE1wjK4pbHB35SjfdNQL1iUYvlI5Qy8V9Wc9W9L4agl%2BzyQvr863o6QiKV4S9aAaOMuC3%2BxYycPa6RtyQfLeGsHake2fVFNgJQdOskcQ7FFwtz3xP7PHiaPRAgkb1OByVgYeQ9PAFf36HBva6SyLP1nQlvH1iw2b4BJ5lSRjKVd8yHxeIVtyFeb6m2l2J7s9OHeQ%2FJwzcxg8cGzcyQQX0nhYobzpt8qlQbv5XVbqXSK7iknEa1wZb%2FGN8F%2BAXZbq28Yd6aq7dj8HfT2haxBqAOjwi8O597seWpHx41Bf%2B0w4B2bdLGXcIUkfYzCXZvTRh5fSJt4xZ6EoTQTowuPCx0gY6mAE7sFBAxiQUWZzmqKtN9vva5JmDd%2BIFIw1l9sTAYcfFojG%2Bt4DzgskOsZ%2FWyr9tI97W%2B8zj7yA26NfpSkxxh%2FV3YMPycyEUA6sGyMIJ6mCBYwhajJPNQo6ZphCHe2I3EhC8FiWHcLtnNPKzYTFHNvZak%2Foz65S%2BoMRRYCS5oY8gfqTg40d2TZFKtbQ5PgICb4Eoe7Oj6hLj5A%3D%3D&Expires=1783399947)

Suggested `frontend/admin-app/src/app/router.tsx`:
```tsx
import { createBrowserRouter, Navigate } from "react-router-dom";
import { AdminLayout } from "../layouts/AdminLayout";
import { AuthLayout } from "../layouts/AuthLayout";
import { LoginPage } from "../pages/LoginPage";
import { DashboardPage } from "../pages/DashboardPage";
import { BillingPage } from "../pages/BillingPage";
import { BackupsPage } from "../pages/BackupsPage";
import { RequireAdminAuth } from "../features/auth/RequireAdminAuth";

export const router = createBrowserRouter([
  {
    path: "/admin/login",
    element: <AuthLayout />,
    children: [{ index: true, element: <LoginPage /> }],
  },
  {
    path: "/admin",
    element: (
      <RequireAdminAuth>
        <AdminLayout />
      </RequireAdminAuth>
    ),
    children: [
      { index: true, element: <DashboardPage /> },
      { path: "billing", element: <BillingPage /> },
      { path: "backups", element: <BackupsPage /> },
    ],
  },
  { path: "*", element: <Navigate to="/admin" replace /> },
]);
```

Suggested `frontend/admin-app/src/lib/http.ts`:
```tsx
export class ApiError extends Error {
  status: number;
  data: unknown;

  constructor(message: string, status: number, data: unknown) {
    super(message);
    this.status = status;
    this.data = data;
  }
}

async function tryRefreshAdminSession() {
  const res = await fetch("/api/admin/refresh", {
    method: "POST",
    credentials: "include",
  });
  return res.ok;
}

export async function apiFetch<T>(
  input: string,
  init: RequestInit = {},
  retry = true
): Promise<T> {
  const res = await fetch(input, {
    ...init,
    credentials: "include",
    headers: {
      "Content-Type": "application/json",
      ...(init.headers || {}),
    },
  });

  const sessionExpired = res.headers.get("X-Session-Expired") === "1";
  const redirectUrl = res.headers.get("X-Redirect-Url");

  if ((res.status === 401 || res.status === 403) && sessionExpired && retry) {
    const refreshed = await tryRefreshAdminSession();
    if (refreshed) {
      return apiFetch<T>(input, init, false);
    }
    window.location.href = redirectUrl || "/admin/login";
    throw new Error("Session expired");
  }

  if (!res.ok) {
    let data: unknown = null;
    try {
      data = await res.json();
    } catch {
      data = await res.text();
    }
    throw new ApiError("Request failed", res.status, data);
  }

  const contentType = res.headers.get("content-type") || "";
  if (contentType.includes("application/json")) {
    return res.json();
  }

  return res.text() as Promise<T>;
}
```

Suggested `frontend/admin-app/src/features/auth/RequireAdminAuth.tsx`:
```tsx
import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
import { Navigate } from "react-router-dom";
import { apiFetch } from "../../lib/http";

export function RequireAdminAuth({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  const [state, setState] = useState<"loading" | "ok" | "no">("loading");

  useEffect(() => {
    apiFetch("/api/admin/me")
      .then(() => setState("ok"))
      .catch(() => setState("no"));
  }, []);

  if (state === "loading") return <div>Loading...</div>;
  if (state === "no") return <Navigate to="/admin/login" replace />;
  return <>{children}</>;
}
```

## First pages

The first three pages should be Login, Dashboard, and Billing, because they establish auth, layout, data fetching, mutations, and file actions. Billing is especially suitable because the backend already exposes bill filtering, preview, creation, updates, payment updates, archive/restore, and PDF endpoints. [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/83904925/d31a7d6a-ed8c-4dfb-9bae-a1aa794ba0bb/rent.md?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQ2J3LGHX&Signature=ZABz0iM%2FzHysP%2FN4QKfuFzmm%2BT8%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEJz%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJHMEUCIQCmQ9rOzLMXAbpPPJ7AJ5PVf6ecWzFa6KIrLAG5jU6x8gIge1jW9GBfqjLBT0RbT4T47sEn7u%2BXJPU1x6qFMf2cMn0q8wQIZRABGgw2OTk3NTMzMDk3MDUiDDuPDwBdT4vFe7d4iirQBLGFc45QATeCwQMpsDtDb9X2wUfVpHpUno%2B6HM7QMoBV4PXMl5KzbtyjVoRBuhrtduYqMJLedKCWLeretbrsvL9priyr4NxxU6iCGbbDagSySm7TyfMWpPWdQaA9VcGIOhsQbs%2FT%2Fe0tPpFVY7uAZo1zyL0ihnqb5d26YlTBzPQwItwYcLW%2BRRF6C1DaIo6ElESlOy86MHuabKS11cuc83dRsXkXUWQAnDlChosGF9P%2F6adV9ZM%2FMfvAe4YbAuWa0VeYhU9WuyuYepSfBatwCnkvGFWWBaBttO0kCUt%2BPGYnFD7TCgeseMsgTGHBQ8UvBp4o73Uxvc41t%2BcJb8sthKytPTd4mN%2BP%2BEDZlmVteBVffPhu42yPN8s4aw8fspqqS9cSLP9%2Bd5NRnnCRLuLtCtMEBMJnRUZCzuqjb%2FluEkvmTl0xpeaXdRcyLDLZQfQ%2F65PmiwELE1wjK4pbHB35SjfdNQL1iUYvlI5Qy8V9Wc9W9L4agl%2BzyQvr863o6QiKV4S9aAaOMuC3%2BxYycPa6RtyQfLeGsHake2fVFNgJQdOskcQ7FFwtz3xP7PHiaPRAgkb1OByVgYeQ9PAFf36HBva6SyLP1nQlvH1iw2b4BJ5lSRjKVd8yHxeIVtyFeb6m2l2J7s9OHeQ%2FJwzcxg8cGzcyQQX0nhYobzpt8qlQbv5XVbqXSK7iknEa1wZb%2FGN8F%2BAXZbq28Yd6aq7dj8HfT2haxBqAOjwi8O597seWpHx41Bf%2B0w4B2bdLGXcIUkfYzCXZvTRh5fSJt4xZ6EoTQTowuPCx0gY6mAE7sFBAxiQUWZzmqKtN9vva5JmDd%2BIFIw1l9sTAYcfFojG%2Bt4DzgskOsZ%2FWyr9tI97W%2B8zj7yA26NfpSkxxh%2FV3YMPycyEUA6sGyMIJ6mCBYwhajJPNQo6ZphCHe2I3EhC8FiWHcLtnNPKzYTFHNvZak%2Foz65S%2BoMRRYCS5oY8gfqTg40d2TZFKtbQ5PgICb4Eoe7Oj6hLj5A%3D%3D&Expires=1783399947)

Suggested `LoginPage.tsx`:
```tsx
import { useState } from "react";
import { useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";

export function LoginPage() {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const [form, setForm] = useState({ username: "", password: "", remember_me: true });
  const [error, setError] = useState("");

  async function onSubmit(e: React.FormEvent) {
    e.preventDefault();
    setError("");

    const res = await fetch("/api/admin/login", {
      method: "POST",
      credentials: "include",
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      body: JSON.stringify(form),
    });

    if (!res.ok) {
      setError("Invalid login");
      return;
    }

    navigate("/admin");
  }

  return (
    <form onSubmit={onSubmit} className="max-w-md mx-auto p-6">
      <h1>Admin Login</h1>
      <input
        placeholder="Username"
        value={form.username}
        onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, username: e.target.value })}
      />
      <input
        placeholder="Password"
        type="password"
        value={form.password}
        onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, password: e.target.value })}
      />
      <label>
        <input
          type="checkbox"
          checked={form.remember_me}
          onChange={(e) => setForm({ ...form, remember_me: e.target.checked })}
        />
        Remember me
      </label>
      <button type="submit">Sign in</button>
      {error && <p>{error}</p>}
    </form>
  );
}
```

Suggested `DashboardPage.tsx`:
```tsx
import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
import { apiFetch } from "../lib/http";

export function DashboardPage() {
  const [data, setData] = useState<any>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    apiFetch<{ status: string; data: any }>("/api/dashboard").then((res) => setData(res.data));
  }, []);

  if (!data) return <div>Loading dashboard...</div>;

  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Dashboard</h1>
      <pre>{JSON.stringify(data, null, 2)}</pre>
    </div>
  );
}
```

Suggested `BillingPage.tsx`:
```tsx
import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
import { apiFetch } from "../lib/http";

export function BillingPage() {
  const [status, setStatus] = useState("active");
  const [rows, setRows] = useState<any[]>([]);

  useEffect(() => {
    apiFetch<any[]>(`/api/bills/filter?status=${status}`).then(setRows);
  }, [status]);

  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Billing</h1>
      <select value={status} onChange={(e) => setStatus(e.target.value)}>
        <option value="active">Active</option>
        <option value="pending">Pending</option>
        <option value="paid">Paid</option>
        <option value="all">All</option>
      </select>

      <table>
        <thead>
          <tr>
            <th>Bill</th>
            <th>Tenant</th>
            <th>Month</th>
            <th>Total</th>
            <th>Payment</th>
            <th>PDF</th>
          </tr>
        </thead>
        <tbody>
          {rows.map((row) => (
            <tr key={row.Bill}>
              <td>{row.Bill}</td>
              <td>{row.Tenant}</td>
              <td>{row.Month}</td>
              <td>{row.Total}</td>
              <td>{row.Payment_Status}</td>
              <td>
                <a href={`/api/pdf/${row.Bill}/view`} target="_blank" rel="noreferrer">
                  View
                </a>
                {" | "}
                <a href={`/api/pdf/${row.Bill}/download`}>
                  Download
                </a>
              </td>
            </tr>
          ))}
        </tbody>
      </table>
    </div>
  );
}
```

## Tenant app starter

The tenant side can also move cleanly to React because login, refresh, logout, logout-all, KYC upload, KYC inactive/delete, and KYC file endpoints already exist. The current tenant login flow is JSON-based at `/api/auth/login`, with refresh at `/api/auth/refresh`, logout at `/api/auth/logout`, and lockout after repeated failed PIN attempts, so React can adopt that flow without reworking the core logic. [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/83904925/d31a7d6a-ed8c-4dfb-9bae-a1aa794ba0bb/rent.md?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQ2J3LGHX&Signature=ZABz0iM%2FzHysP%2FN4QKfuFzmm%2BT8%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEJz%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJHMEUCIQCmQ9rOzLMXAbpPPJ7AJ5PVf6ecWzFa6KIrLAG5jU6x8gIge1jW9GBfqjLBT0RbT4T47sEn7u%2BXJPU1x6qFMf2cMn0q8wQIZRABGgw2OTk3NTMzMDk3MDUiDDuPDwBdT4vFe7d4iirQBLGFc45QATeCwQMpsDtDb9X2wUfVpHpUno%2B6HM7QMoBV4PXMl5KzbtyjVoRBuhrtduYqMJLedKCWLeretbrsvL9priyr4NxxU6iCGbbDagSySm7TyfMWpPWdQaA9VcGIOhsQbs%2FT%2Fe0tPpFVY7uAZo1zyL0ihnqb5d26YlTBzPQwItwYcLW%2BRRF6C1DaIo6ElESlOy86MHuabKS11cuc83dRsXkXUWQAnDlChosGF9P%2F6adV9ZM%2FMfvAe4YbAuWa0VeYhU9WuyuYepSfBatwCnkvGFWWBaBttO0kCUt%2BPGYnFD7TCgeseMsgTGHBQ8UvBp4o73Uxvc41t%2BcJb8sthKytPTd4mN%2BP%2BEDZlmVteBVffPhu42yPN8s4aw8fspqqS9cSLP9%2Bd5NRnnCRLuLtCtMEBMJnRUZCzuqjb%2FluEkvmTl0xpeaXdRcyLDLZQfQ%2F65PmiwELE1wjK4pbHB35SjfdNQL1iUYvlI5Qy8V9Wc9W9L4agl%2BzyQvr863o6QiKV4S9aAaOMuC3%2BxYycPa6RtyQfLeGsHake2fVFNgJQdOskcQ7FFwtz3xP7PHiaPRAgkb1OByVgYeQ9PAFf36HBva6SyLP1nQlvH1iw2b4BJ5lSRjKVd8yHxeIVtyFeb6m2l2J7s9OHeQ%2FJwzcxg8cGzcyQQX0nhYobzpt8qlQbv5XVbqXSK7iknEa1wZb%2FGN8F%2BAXZbq28Yd6aq7dj8HfT2haxBqAOjwi8O597seWpHx41Bf%2B0w4B2bdLGXcIUkfYzCXZvTRh5fSJt4xZ6EoTQTowuPCx0gY6mAE7sFBAxiQUWZzmqKtN9vva5JmDd%2BIFIw1l9sTAYcfFojG%2Bt4DzgskOsZ%2FWyr9tI97W%2B8zj7yA26NfpSkxxh%2FV3YMPycyEUA6sGyMIJ6mCBYwhajJPNQo6ZphCHe2I3EhC8FiWHcLtnNPKzYTFHNvZak%2Foz65S%2BoMRRYCS5oY8gfqTg40d2TZFKtbQ5PgICb4Eoe7Oj6hLj5A%3D%3D&Expires=1783399947)

Suggested tenant router:
```tsx
import { createBrowserRouter } from "react-router-dom";
import { PublicTenantPage } from "../pages/PublicTenantPage";

export const router = createBrowserRouter([
  {
    path: "/t/:viewToken",
    element: <PublicTenantPage />,
  },
]);
```

Suggested `PublicTenantPage.tsx`:
```tsx
import { useParams } from "react-router-dom";
import { useEffect, useState } from "react";

export function PublicTenantPage() {
  const { viewToken = "" } = useParams();
  const [pin, setPin] = useState("");
  const [tenant, setTenant] = useState<any>(null);
  const [loggedIn, setLoggedIn] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState("");

  useEffect(() => {
    fetch(`/api/public/tenant/${viewToken}`, { credentials: "include" })
      .then((r) => r.json())
      .then((d) => setTenant(d.tenant))
      .catch(() => setError("Invalid profile link"));
  }, [viewToken]);

  async function login() {
    setError("");
    const res = await fetch("/api/auth/login", {
      method: "POST",
      credentials: "include",
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      body: JSON.stringify({ view_token: viewToken, pin, remember_me: true }),
    });

    if (!res.ok) {
      const data = await res.json().catch(() => null);
      setError(data?.detail || "Login failed");
      return;
    }

    setLoggedIn(true);
  }

  if (!tenant) return <div>Loading...</div>;

  return (
    <div>
      <h1>{tenant.name}</h1>
      {!loggedIn ? (
        <div>
          <input
            type="password"
            placeholder="Enter PIN"
            value={pin}
            onChange={(e) => setPin(e.target.value)}
          />
          <button onClick={login}>Unlock</button>
          {error && <p>{error}</p>}
        </div>
      ) : (
        <div>Tenant portal unlocked</div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
```

## Backend endpoints to add now

Add only the minimum new endpoints needed for React bootstrap, because your existing APIs already cover most actions. The most important additions are `GET /api/admin/me`, `POST /api/admin/login`, `POST /api/admin/logout`, `POST /api/admin/refresh`, `GET /api/dashboard`, `GET /api/public/tenant/{view_token}`, and `GET /api/auth/me`. [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/83904925/d31a7d6a-ed8c-4dfb-9bae-a1aa794ba0bb/rent.md?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEQ2J3LGHX&Signature=ZABz0iM%2FzHysP%2FN4QKfuFzmm%2BT8%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEJz%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJHMEUCIQCmQ9rOzLMXAbpPPJ7AJ5PVf6ecWzFa6KIrLAG5jU6x8gIge1jW9GBfqjLBT0RbT4T47sEn7u%2BXJPU1x6qFMf2cMn0q8wQIZRABGgw2OTk3NTMzMDk3MDUiDDuPDwBdT4vFe7d4iirQBLGFc45QATeCwQMpsDtDb9X2wUfVpHpUno%2B6HM7QMoBV4PXMl5KzbtyjVoRBuhrtduYqMJLedKCWLeretbrsvL9priyr4NxxU6iCGbbDagSySm7TyfMWpPWdQaA9VcGIOhsQbs%2FT%2Fe0tPpFVY7uAZo1zyL0ihnqb5d26YlTBzPQwItwYcLW%2BRRF6C1DaIo6ElESlOy86MHuabKS11cuc83dRsXkXUWQAnDlChosGF9P%2F6adV9ZM%2FMfvAe4YbAuWa0VeYhU9WuyuYepSfBatwCnkvGFWWBaBttO0kCUt%2BPGYnFD7TCgeseMsgTGHBQ8UvBp4o73Uxvc41t%2BcJb8sthKytPTd4mN%2BP%2BEDZlmVteBVffPhu42yPN8s4aw8fspqqS9cSLP9%2Bd5NRnnCRLuLtCtMEBMJnRUZCzuqjb%2FluEkvmTl0xpeaXdRcyLDLZQfQ%2F65PmiwELE1wjK4pbHB35SjfdNQL1iUYvlI5Qy8V9Wc9W9L4agl%2BzyQvr863o6QiKV4S9aAaOMuC3%2BxYycPa6RtyQfLeGsHake2fVFNgJQdOskcQ7FFwtz3xP7PHiaPRAgkb1OByVgYeQ9PAFf36HBva6SyLP1nQlvH1iw2b4BJ5lSRjKVd8yHxeIVtyFeb6m2l2J7s9OHeQ%2FJwzcxg8cGzcyQQX0nhYobzpt8qlQbv5XVbqXSK7iknEa1wZb%2FGN8F%2BAXZbq28Yd6aq7dj8HfT2haxBqAOjwi8O597seWpHx41Bf%2B0w4B2bdLGXcIUkfYzCXZvTRh5fSJt4xZ6EoTQTowuPCx0gY6mAE7sFBAxiQUWZzmqKtN9vva5JmDd%2BIFIw1l9sTAYcfFojG%2Bt4DzgskOsZ%2FWyr9tI97W%2B8zj7yA26NfpSkxxh%2FV3YMPycyEUA6sGyMIJ6mCBYwhajJPNQo6ZphCHe2I3EhC8FiWHcLtnNPKzYTFHNvZak%2Foz65S%2BoMRRYCS5oY8gfqTg40d2TZFKtbQ5PgICb4Eoe7Oj6hLj5A%3D%3D&Expires=1783399947)

## Rollout order

The best sequence is:
1. Add new JSON bootstrap/auth endpoints.
2. Build admin login, dashboard, and billing in React.
3. Switch `/admin` to serve the React app.
4. Migrate tenants, settings, archive, backups, and sync.
5. Migrate `/t/{view_token}` to the React tenant app.
6. Remove old template pages after parity testing. This staged rollout reduces risk because backups, billing, PDFs, and tenant auth already function through backend endpoints, so you are mainly replacing rendering and interaction layers rather than business logic.
